      <div role="note" class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable">
       This article is about the country. For other uses, see <a href="/wiki/Palau_(disambiguation)" class="mw-disambig" title="Palau (disambiguation)">Palau (disambiguation)</a>.
      </div> 
      <div role="note" class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable">
       Not to be confused with <a href="/wiki/Paelau" title="Paelau">Paelau</a>.
      </div>

       "Belau" redirects here. For the municipality in Germany, see <a href="/wiki/Belau,_Schleswig-Holstein" title="Belau, Schleswig-Holstein">Belau, Schleswig-Holstein</a>.
      </div>

       Country in the western Pacific

      <p><b>Palau</b> (<span class="rt-commentedText nowrap"><span class="IPA nopopups noexcerpt"><a href="/wiki/Help:IPA/English" title="Help:IPA/English">/<span style="border-bottom:1px dotted"><span title="'p' in 'pie'">p</span><span title="/ə/: 'a' in 'about'">ə</span><span title="/ˈ/: primary stress follows">ˈ</span><span title="'l' in 'lie'">l</span><span title="/aʊ/: 'ou' in 'mouth'">aʊ</span></span>/</a></span> <span class="nowrap" style="font-size:85%">(<span class="unicode haudio"><span class="fn"><span style="white-space:nowrap;margin-right:.25em;"><a href="/wiki/File:En-us-Palau.ogg" title="About this sound"><img alt="About this sound" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/8/8a/Loudspeaker.svg/11px-Loudspeaker.svg.png" decoding="async" width="11" height="11" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/8/8a/Loudspeaker.svg/17px-Loudspeaker.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/8/8a/Loudspeaker.svg/22px-Loudspeaker.svg.png 2x" data-file-width="20" data-file-height="20"></a></span><a href="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/e/ea/En-us-Palau.ogg" class="internal" title="En-us-Palau.ogg">listen</a></span></span>)</span></span>), officially the <b>Republic of Palau</b> (<a href="/wiki/Palauan_language" title="Palauan language">Palauan</a>: <i lang="pau">Beluu er a Belau</i>)<sup id="cite_ref-7" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-7">[7]</a></sup> and historically <i>Belau</i>, <i>Palaos</i> or <i>Pelew</i>, is an <a href="/wiki/Island_country" title="Island country">island country</a> in the western <a href="/wiki/Pacific_Ocean" title="Pacific Ocean">Pacific</a>. The nation has approximately 340 islands and connects the western chain of the <a href="/wiki/Caroline_Islands" title="Caroline Islands">Caroline Islands</a> with parts of the <a href="/wiki/Federated_States_of_Micronesia" title="Federated States of Micronesia">Federated States of Micronesia</a>. It has a total area of 466 square kilometers (180 square miles).<sup id="cite_ref-8" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-8">[8]</a></sup> The most populous island is <a href="/wiki/Koror" title="Koror">Koror</a>. The capital <a href="/wiki/Ngerulmud" title="Ngerulmud">Ngerulmud</a> is located on the nearby island of <a href="/wiki/Babeldaob" title="Babeldaob">Babeldaob</a>, in <a href="/wiki/Melekeok" title="Melekeok">Melekeok State</a>. Palau shares <a href="/wiki/Maritime_boundary" title="Maritime boundary">maritime boundaries</a> with <a href="/wiki/International_waters" title="International waters">international waters</a> to the north, <a href="/wiki/Federated_States_of_Micronesia" title="Federated States of Micronesia">Micronesia</a> to the east, <a href="/wiki/Indonesia" title="Indonesia">Indonesia</a> to the south, and the <a href="/wiki/Philippines" title="Philippines">Philippines</a> to the north west. </p>
      <p>The country was originally settled approximately 3,000 years ago by migrants from <a href="/wiki/Maritime_Southeast_Asia" title="Maritime Southeast Asia">Maritime Southeast Asia</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-9" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-9">[9]</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-SmithWMP_10-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-SmithWMP-10">[10]</a></sup> Spain was the first European nation to explore the islands in the 16th century, and they were made part of the <a href="/wiki/Spanish_East_Indies" title="Spanish East Indies">Spanish East Indies</a> in 1574. Following Spain's defeat in the <a href="/wiki/Spanish%E2%80%93American_War" title="Spanish–American War">Spanish–American War</a> in 1898, the islands were sold to <a href="/wiki/Imperial_Germany" class="mw-redirect" title="Imperial Germany">Imperial Germany</a> in 1899 under the terms of the <a href="/wiki/German%E2%80%93Spanish_Treaty_(1899)" title="German–Spanish Treaty (1899)">German–Spanish Treaty</a>, where they were administered as part of <a href="/wiki/German_New_Guinea" title="German New Guinea">German New Guinea</a>. After <a href="/wiki/World_War_I" title="World War I">World War I</a>, the islands were made a part of the Japanese-ruled <a href="/wiki/South_Seas_Mandate" title="South Seas Mandate">South Seas Mandate</a> by the <a href="/wiki/League_of_Nations" title="League of Nations">League of Nations</a>. During <a href="/wiki/World_War_II" title="World War II">World War II</a>, skirmishes, including the major <a href="/wiki/Battle_of_Peleliu" title="Battle of Peleliu">Battle of Peleliu</a>, were fought between American and Japanese troops as part of the <a href="/wiki/Mariana_and_Palau_Islands_campaign" title="Mariana and Palau Islands campaign">Mariana and Palau Islands campaign</a>. Along with other <a href="/wiki/List_of_islands_in_the_Pacific_Ocean" title="List of islands in the Pacific Ocean">Pacific Islands</a>, Palau was made a part of the United States-governed <a href="/wiki/Trust_Territory_of_the_Pacific_Islands" title="Trust Territory of the Pacific Islands">Trust Territory of the Pacific Islands</a> in <a href="/wiki/1947" title="1947">1947</a>. Having voted against joining the Federated States of Micronesia in 1979, the islands gained full <a href="/wiki/Sovereignty" title="Sovereignty">sovereignty</a> in 1994 under a <a href="/wiki/Compact_of_Free_Association" title="Compact of Free Association">Compact of Free Association</a> with the United States. </p>
      <p>Politically, Palau is a <a href="/wiki/Presidential_system" title="Presidential system">presidential</a> <a href="/wiki/Republic" title="Republic">republic</a> in <a href="/wiki/Associated_state" title="Associated state">free association</a> with the United States, which provides defense, funding, and access to social services. Legislative power is concentrated in the <a href="/wiki/Bicameral" class="mw-redirect" title="Bicameral">bicameral</a> <a href="/wiki/Palau_National_Congress" title="Palau National Congress">Palau National Congress</a>. <a href="/wiki/Economy_of_Palau" title="Economy of Palau">Palau's economy</a> is based mainly on <a href="/wiki/Tourism" title="Tourism">tourism</a>, <a href="/wiki/Subsistence_agriculture" title="Subsistence agriculture">subsistence agriculture</a> and <a href="/wiki/Fishing" title="Fishing">fishing</a>, with a significant portion of <a href="/wiki/Gross_national_product" class="mw-redirect" title="Gross national product">gross national product</a> (GNP) derived from foreign aid. The country uses the <a href="/wiki/United_States_dollar" title="United States dollar">United States dollar</a> as its currency. The islands' culture mixes Micronesian, <a href="/wiki/Melanesia" title="Melanesia">Melanesian</a>, Asian, and Western elements. Ethnic Palauans, the majority of the population, are of mixed Micronesian, Melanesian, and <a href="/wiki/Austronesia" class="mw-redirect" title="Austronesia">Austronesian</a> descent. A smaller proportion of the population is of <a href="/wiki/Japanese_people" title="Japanese people">Japanese</a> descent. The country's two <a href="/wiki/Official_language" title="Official language">official languages</a> are <a href="/wiki/Palauan_language" title="Palauan language">Palauan</a> (a member of the <a href="/wiki/Austronesian_languages" title="Austronesian languages">Austronesian</a> language family) and <a href="/wiki/English_language" title="English language">English</a>, with <a href="/wiki/Japanese_language" title="Japanese language">Japanese</a>, <a href="/wiki/Sonsorolese_language" title="Sonsorolese language">Sonsorolese</a>, and <a href="/wiki/Tobian_language" title="Tobian language">Tobian</a> recognized as <a href="/wiki/Regional_language" title="Regional language">regional languages</a>. </p>

          <li class="toclevel-2 tocsection-31"><a href="#Government"><span class="tocnumber">11.1</span> <span class="toctext">Government</span></a></li> 
          <li class="toclevel-2 tocsection-32"><a href="#Local_News"><span class="tocnumber">11.2</span> <span class="toctext">Local News</span></a></li> 
          <li class="toclevel-2 tocsection-33"><a href="#General_information"><span class="tocnumber">11.3</span> <span class="toctext">General information</span></a></li> 
         </ul> </li>

      </div> 
      <h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Palau&amp;action=edit&amp;section=1" title="Edit section: Etymology">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2> 
      <p>The name for the islands in the <a href="/wiki/Palauan_language" title="Palauan language">Palauan language</a>, <i>Belau</i>, derives from the Palauan word for "village", <i>beluu</i>,<sup id="cite_ref-11" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-11">[11]</a></sup> or from <i>aibebelau</i> ("indirect replies"), relating to a <a href="/wiki/Creation_myth" title="Creation myth">creation myth</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-12" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-12">[12]</a></sup> The name "Palau" entered the <a href="/wiki/English_language" title="English language">English language</a> from the <a href="/wiki/Spanish_language" title="Spanish language">Spanish</a> <i>Los Palaos</i>, via the <a href="/wiki/German_language" title="German language">German</a> <i>Palau</i>. An archaic name for the islands in English was the "Pelew Islands".<sup id="cite_ref-13" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-13">[13]</a></sup> <i>Palau</i> is unrelated to <i>Pulau</i>, which is a <a href="/wiki/Malay_language" title="Malay language">Malay</a> word meaning "island" found in a number of place names in the region. </p> 
      <h2><span class="mw-headline" id="History">History</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Palau&amp;action=edit&amp;section=2" title="Edit section: History">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2> 
      <div role="note" class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable">

      <h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Early_history">Early history</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Palau&amp;action=edit&amp;section=3" title="Edit section: Early history">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3> 
      <link rel="mw-deduplicated-inline-style" href="mw-data:TemplateStyles:r992277484">
      <div class="mw-stack stack-container stack-right">
       <div>
        <div class="thumb tright">
         <div class="thumbinner" style="width:292px;">
          <a href="/wiki/File:Reception_of_the_Manila_Galleon_by_the_Chamorro_in_the_Ladrones_Islands,_ca._1590.jpg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/6d/Reception_of_the_Manila_Galleon_by_the_Chamorro_in_the_Ladrones_Islands%2C_ca._1590.jpg/290px-Reception_of_the_Manila_Galleon_by_the_Chamorro_in_the_Ladrones_Islands%2C_ca._1590.jpg" decoding="async" width="290" height="92" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/6d/Reception_of_the_Manila_Galleon_by_the_Chamorro_in_the_Ladrones_Islands%2C_ca._1590.jpg/435px-Reception_of_the_Manila_Galleon_by_the_Chamorro_in_the_Ladrones_Islands%2C_ca._1590.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/6d/Reception_of_the_Manila_Galleon_by_the_Chamorro_in_the_Ladrones_Islands%2C_ca._1590.jpg/580px-Reception_of_the_Manila_Galleon_by_the_Chamorro_in_the_Ladrones_Islands%2C_ca._1590.jpg 2x" data-file-width="937" data-file-height="298"></a> 
          <div class="thumbcaption">
           <div class="magnify">
            <a href="/wiki/File:Reception_of_the_Manila_Galleon_by_the_Chamorro_in_the_Ladrones_Islands,_ca._1590.jpg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a>
           </div><a href="/wiki/Manila_galleon" title="Manila galleon">Manila Galleon</a> in the <a href="/wiki/Mariana_Islands" title="Mariana Islands">Marianas</a> and <a href="/wiki/Caroline_Islands" title="Caroline Islands">Carolinas</a>, c. 1590 <a href="/wiki/Boxer_Codex" title="Boxer Codex">Boxer Codex</a>.
          </div>
         </div>
        </div>
       </div>
      </div> 
      <p>Palau was originally settled between the <a href="/wiki/3rd_millennium_BCE" class="mw-redirect" title="3rd millennium BCE">3rd</a> and <a href="/wiki/2nd_millennium_BCE" class="mw-redirect" title="2nd millennium BCE">2nd millennia BCE</a>, most likely from the <a href="/wiki/Philippines" title="Philippines">Philippines</a> or <a href="/wiki/Indonesia" title="Indonesia">Indonesia</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-14" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-14">[14]</a></sup> <a href="/wiki/Sonsorol" title="Sonsorol">Sonsorol</a>, part of the <a href="/wiki/Southwest_Islands_(Palau)" title="Southwest Islands (Palau)">Southwest Islands</a>, an island chain approximately 600 kilometers (370&nbsp;mi; 320&nbsp;nmi) from the main island chain of Palau, was sighted by the <a href="/wiki/Spanish_Empire" title="Spanish Empire">Spanish</a> as early as 1522, when the <a href="/wiki/Spanish_missions_in_the_Carolinas" title="Spanish missions in the Carolinas">Spanish mission</a> of the <i><a href="/wiki/Trinidad_(ship)" title="Trinidad (ship)">Trinidad</a></i>, the flagship of <a href="/wiki/Ferdinand_Magellan" title="Ferdinand Magellan">Ferdinand Magellan</a>'s voyage of circumnavigation, sighted two small islands around the <a href="/wiki/5th_parallel_north" title="5th parallel north">5th parallel north</a>, naming them "San Juan".<sup id="cite_ref-15" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-15">[15]</a></sup> </p> 
      <h3><span class="mw-headline" id="After_the_16th_century">After the 16th century</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Palau&amp;action=edit&amp;section=4" title="Edit section: After the 16th century">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3> 
      <p>The next recording of the existence of Palau by Europeans came a century later in 1697 when a group of Palauans were shipwrecked on the Philippine island of <a href="/wiki/Samar" title="Samar">Samar</a> to the northwest. They were interviewed by the <a href="/wiki/Czechs" title="Czechs">Czech</a> missionary <a href="/wiki/Pablo_Clain" title="Pablo Clain">Paul Klein</a> on 28 December 1696. Klein was able to draw the first map of Palau based on the Palauans' representation of their home islands that they made with an arrangement of 87 pebbles on the beach . Klein reported his findings to the <a href="/wiki/Superior_General_of_the_Society_of_Jesus" title="Superior General of the Society of Jesus">Jesuit Superior General</a> in a letter sent in June 1697.<sup id="cite_ref-16" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-16">[16]</a></sup> </p> 
      <h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Spanish_era">Spanish era</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Palau&amp;action=edit&amp;section=5" title="Edit section: Spanish era">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3> 
      <div role="note" class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable">
       Main articles: <a href="/wiki/New_Spain" title="New Spain">New Spain</a>, <a href="/wiki/Captaincy_General_of_the_Philippines" title="Captaincy General of the Philippines">Captaincy General of the Philippines</a>, and <a href="/wiki/Spanish_East_Indies" title="Spanish East Indies">Spanish East Indies</a>
      </div> 
      <link rel="mw-deduplicated-inline-style" href="mw-data:TemplateStyles:r992277484">
      <div class="mw-stack stack-container stack-right">
       <div> 
        <div class="thumb tright">
         <div class="thumbinner" style="width:332px;">
          <a href="/wiki/File:Islas_Marianas_Palaos_y_Carolinas.JPG" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/e/e4/Islas_Marianas_Palaos_y_Carolinas.JPG/330px-Islas_Marianas_Palaos_y_Carolinas.JPG" decoding="async" width="330" height="179" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/e/e4/Islas_Marianas_Palaos_y_Carolinas.JPG/495px-Islas_Marianas_Palaos_y_Carolinas.JPG 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/e/e4/Islas_Marianas_Palaos_y_Carolinas.JPG/660px-Islas_Marianas_Palaos_y_Carolinas.JPG 2x" data-file-width="902" data-file-height="489"></a> 
          <div class="thumbcaption">
           <div class="magnify">
            <a href="/wiki/File:Islas_Marianas_Palaos_y_Carolinas.JPG" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a>
           </div>An 1888 map showing the Palau Islands of the Spanish East Indies (excluding the Philippine Islands).
          </div>
         </div>
        </div> 
        <div class="thumb tright">
         <div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;">
          <a href="/wiki/File:Palau-Inseln.jpg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/9/9e/Palau-Inseln.jpg/220px-Palau-Inseln.jpg" decoding="async" width="220" height="128" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/9/9e/Palau-Inseln.jpg/330px-Palau-Inseln.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/9/9e/Palau-Inseln.jpg/440px-Palau-Inseln.jpg 2x" data-file-width="681" data-file-height="395"></a> 
          <div class="thumbcaption">
           <div class="magnify">
            <a href="/wiki/File:Palau-Inseln.jpg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a>
           </div>Palau under German rule; painting by <a href="/wiki/Rudolf_Hellgrewe" title="Rudolf Hellgrewe">Rudolf Hellgrewe</a> c. 1908.
          </div>
         </div>
        </div> 
        <div class="thumb tright">
         <div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;">
          <a href="/wiki/File:Koror_chiefs_in_1915.jpg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/5/5b/Koror_chiefs_in_1915.jpg/220px-Koror_chiefs_in_1915.jpg" decoding="async" width="220" height="164" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/5/5b/Koror_chiefs_in_1915.jpg/330px-Koror_chiefs_in_1915.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/5/5b/Koror_chiefs_in_1915.jpg/440px-Koror_chiefs_in_1915.jpg 2x" data-file-width="472" data-file-height="352"></a> 
          <div class="thumbcaption">
           <div class="magnify">
            <a href="/wiki/File:Koror_chiefs_in_1915.jpg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a>
           </div>Koror chiefs in 1915.
          </div>
         </div>
        </div> 
       </div>
      </div> 
      <p>This map and the letter caused a vast interest in the new islands. Another letter written by Fr. Andrés Serrano was sent to Europe in 1705, essentially copying the information given by Klein. The letters resulted in three unsuccessful Jesuit attempts to travel to Palau from <a href="/wiki/Spanish_Philippines" class="mw-redirect" title="Spanish Philippines">Spanish Philippines</a> in 1700, 1708 and 1709. The islands were first visited by the Jesuit expedition led by Francisco Padilla on 30 November 1710. The expedition ended with the stranding of the two priests, Jacques Du Beron and Joseph Cortyl, on the coast of Sonsorol, because the mother ship <i><a href="/wiki/Trinity" title="Trinity">Santísima Trinidad</a></i> was driven to <a href="/wiki/Mindanao" title="Mindanao">Mindanao</a> by a storm. Another ship was sent from <a href="/wiki/Guam" title="Guam">Guam</a> in 1711 to save them only to capsize, causing the death of three more Jesuit priests. The failure of these missions gave Palau the original Spanish name <i>Islas Encantadas</i> (Enchanted Islands).<sup id="cite_ref-17" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-17">[17]</a></sup> Despite these early misfortunes, the <a href="/wiki/Spanish_Empire" title="Spanish Empire">Spanish Empire</a> later came to dominate the islands.<sup class="noprint Inline-Template Template-Fact" style="white-space:nowrap;">[<i><a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Citation_needed" title="Wikipedia:Citation needed"><span title="This claim needs references to reliable sources. (April 2021)">citation needed</span></a></i>]</sup> </p> 
      <h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Transitions_era">Transitions era</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Palau&amp;action=edit&amp;section=6" title="Edit section: Transitions era">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3> 
      <p>British traders became regular visitors to Palau in the 18th century, followed by expanding Spanish influence in the 19th century. Palau, under the name <i>Palaos</i>, was included in the <a href="/wiki/Malolos_Congress" title="Malolos Congress">Malolos Congress</a> in 1898, the first revolutionary congress in the <a href="/wiki/Philippines" title="Philippines">Philippines</a>, which wanted full independence from colonialists. Palau, at the time, was part of the <a href="/wiki/Spanish_East_Indies" title="Spanish East Indies">Spanish East Indies</a> headquartered in the <a href="/wiki/Captaincy_General_of_the_Philippines" title="Captaincy General of the Philippines">Philippines</a>. Palau had one appointed member to the Congress, becoming the only group of islands in the entire Caroline Islands granted high representation in a non-colonial Philippine Congress. The Congress also supported the right of Palau to self-determination if ever it wished to pursue such a path.<sup id="cite_ref-PhilStar2006_18-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-PhilStar2006-18">[18]</a></sup> Later in 1899 as part of the <a href="/wiki/Caroline_Islands" title="Caroline Islands">Caroline Islands</a>, Palau was sold by the <a href="/wiki/Spanish_Empire" title="Spanish Empire">Spanish Empire</a> to the <a href="/wiki/German_Empire" title="German Empire">German Empire</a> as part of <a href="/wiki/German_New_Guinea" title="German New Guinea">German New Guinea</a> in the <a href="/wiki/German%E2%80%93Spanish_Treaty_(1899)" title="German–Spanish Treaty (1899)">German–Spanish Treaty (1899)</a>. During <a href="/wiki/World_War_I" title="World War I">World War I</a>, the <a href="/wiki/Empire_of_Japan" title="Empire of Japan">Japanese Empire</a> annexed the islands after seizing them from <a href="/wiki/German_Empire" title="German Empire">Germany</a> in 1914. Following World War I, the <a href="/wiki/League_of_Nations" title="League of Nations">League of Nations</a> formally placed the islands under Japanese administration as part of the <a href="/wiki/South_Seas_Mandate" title="South Seas Mandate">South Seas Mandate</a>. In World War II, Palau was used by Japan to support its <a href="/wiki/Philippines_campaign_(1941%E2%80%931942)" class="mw-redirect" title="Philippines campaign (1941–1942)">1941 invasion of the Philippines</a>, which succeeded in 1942. The invasion overthrew the American-installed <a href="/wiki/Commonwealth_of_the_Philippines" title="Commonwealth of the Philippines">Commonwealth government in the Philippines</a> and installed the Japanese-backed <a href="/wiki/Second_Philippine_Republic" title="Second Philippine Republic">Second Philippine Republic</a> in 1943.<sup id="cite_ref-19" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-19">[19]</a></sup> </p> 
      <h3><span class="mw-headline" id="United_States_era">United States era</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Palau&amp;action=edit&amp;section=7" title="Edit section: United States era">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3> 
      <p>During <a href="/wiki/World_War_II" title="World War II">World War II</a>, the United States captured Palau from Japan in 1944 after the costly <a href="/wiki/Battle_of_Peleliu" title="Battle of Peleliu">Battle of Peleliu</a>, when more than 2,000 Americans and 10,000 Japanese were killed. In 1945–1946, the United States re-established control on the <a href="/wiki/Philippines" title="Philippines">Philippines</a>, and managed Palau through the Philippine capital of <a href="/wiki/Manila" title="Manila">Manila</a>. By the later half of 1946, however, the Philippines was granted full independence with the formation of the <a href="/wiki/Third_Republic_of_the_Philippines" class="mw-redirect" title="Third Republic of the Philippines">Third Republic of the Philippines</a>, shifting the US Far West Pacific capital to <a href="/wiki/Guam" title="Guam">Guam</a>. Palau passed formally to the United States under <a href="/wiki/United_Nations" title="United Nations">United Nations</a> auspices in 1947 as part of the <a href="/wiki/Trust_Territory_of_the_Pacific_Islands" title="Trust Territory of the Pacific Islands">Trust Territory of the Pacific Islands</a> established pursuant to <a href="/wiki/United_Nations_Security_Council_Resolution_21" title="United Nations Security Council Resolution 21">Security Council Resolution 21</a>.<sup class="noprint Inline-Template Template-Fact" style="white-space:nowrap;">[<i><a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Citation_needed" title="Wikipedia:Citation needed"><span title="This claim needs references to reliable sources. (April 2021)">citation needed</span></a></i>]</sup> </p> 
      <h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Independence">Independence</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Palau&amp;action=edit&amp;section=8" title="Edit section: Independence">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3> 
      <link rel="mw-deduplicated-inline-style" href="mw-data:TemplateStyles:r992277484">
      <div class="mw-stack stack-container stack-right">
       <div>
        <div class="thumb tright">
         <div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;">
          <a href="/wiki/File:TTPI_High_Commissioner_and_staff.jpg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/4/40/TTPI_High_Commissioner_and_staff.jpg/220px-TTPI_High_Commissioner_and_staff.jpg" decoding="async" width="220" height="154" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/4/40/TTPI_High_Commissioner_and_staff.jpg/330px-TTPI_High_Commissioner_and_staff.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/4/40/TTPI_High_Commissioner_and_staff.jpg/440px-TTPI_High_Commissioner_and_staff.jpg 2x" data-file-width="640" data-file-height="449"></a> 
          <div class="thumbcaption">
           <div class="magnify">
            <a href="/wiki/File:TTPI_High_Commissioner_and_staff.jpg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a>
           </div>TTPI High Commissioner and staff, 1960s.
          </div>
         </div>
        </div>
       </div>
      </div> 
      <p>Four of the Trust Territory districts joined together and formed the <a href="/wiki/Federated_States_of_Micronesia" title="Federated States of Micronesia">Federated States of Micronesia</a> in 1979, but the districts of Palau and the <a href="/wiki/Marshall_Islands" title="Marshall Islands">Marshall Islands</a> declined to participate. Palau, the westernmost cluster of the <a href="/wiki/Caroline_Islands" title="Caroline Islands">Carolines</a>, instead opted for independent status in 1978, which was widely supported by the <a href="/wiki/Philippines" title="Philippines">Philippines</a>, <a href="/wiki/Taiwan" title="Taiwan">Taiwan</a>, and <a href="/wiki/Japan" title="Japan">Japan</a>. It approved a new constitution and became the Republic of Palau on 1 January 1981.<sup id="cite_ref-20" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-20">[20]</a></sup> It signed a <a href="/wiki/Compact_of_Free_Association" title="Compact of Free Association">Compact of Free Association</a> with the United States in 1982. In the same year, Palau became one of the founding members of the <a href="/wiki/Nauru_Agreement" title="Nauru Agreement">Nauru Agreement</a>. After eight referenda and an amendment to the Palauan constitution, the Compact was ratified in 1993. The Compact went into effect on 1 October 1994,<sup id="cite_ref-21" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-21">[21]</a></sup> making Palau <i><a href="/wiki/De_jure" title="De jure">de jure</a></i> independent, although it had been <i><a href="/wiki/De_facto" title="De facto">de facto</a></i> independent since 25 May 1994, when the trusteeship ended. Formal diplomatic relations with the <a href="/wiki/Philippines" title="Philippines">Philippines</a> was re-established in the same year, although the two nations already had diplomatic back channels prior to 1994.<sup class="noprint Inline-Template Template-Fact" style="white-space:nowrap;">[<i><a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Citation_needed" title="Wikipedia:Citation needed"><span title="This claim needs references to reliable sources. (May 2018)">citation needed</span></a></i>]</sup> Palau also became a member of the <a href="/wiki/Pacific_Islands_Forum" title="Pacific Islands Forum">Pacific Islands Forum</a>, but withdrew in February 2021 after a dispute regarding <a href="/wiki/Henry_Puna" title="Henry Puna">Henry Puna</a>'s election as the Forum's secretary-general.<sup id="cite_ref-22" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-22">[22]</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-23" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-23">[23]</a></sup> </p>
      <p>Legislation making Palau an "offshore" financial center was passed by the <a href="/wiki/US_Senate" class="mw-redirect" title="US Senate">US Senate</a> in 1998.<sup class="noprint Inline-Template Template-Fact" style="white-space:nowrap;">[<i><a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Citation_needed" title="Wikipedia:Citation needed"><span title="This claim needs references to reliable sources. (April 2021)">citation needed</span></a></i>]</sup> </p>
      <p>In 2001, Palau passed its first <a href="/wiki/Bank_regulation" title="Bank regulation">bank regulation</a> and anti-<a href="/wiki/Money_laundering" title="Money laundering">money laundering</a> laws.<sup class="noprint Inline-Template Template-Fact" style="white-space:nowrap;">[<i><a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Citation_needed" title="Wikipedia:Citation needed"><span title="This claim needs references to reliable sources. (April 2021)">citation needed</span></a></i>]</sup> </p>
      <p>In 2005, Palau led the <a href="/wiki/Micronesia_challenge" class="mw-redirect" title="Micronesia challenge">Micronesia challenge</a>, which would conserve 30% of near-shore coastal waters and 20% of forest land of participating countries by 2020. In 2011, Palau created the world's first <a href="/wiki/Shark_sanctuary" title="Shark sanctuary">shark sanctuary</a>, banning commercial shark fishing within its waters. In 2012, the <a href="/wiki/Rock_Islands" title="Rock Islands">Rock Islands</a> of Palau was declared as a <a href="/wiki/UNESCO" title="UNESCO">UNESCO</a> <a href="/wiki/World_Heritage_Site" title="World Heritage Site">World Heritage Site</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-24" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-24">[24]</a></sup> </p>
      <p>In 2015, Palau became a member of the <a href="/wiki/Climate_Vulnerable_Forum" title="Climate Vulnerable Forum">Climate Vulnerable Forum</a> under the chairmanship of the Philippines, and at the same time, the country officially protected 80% of its water resources, becoming the first country to do so.<sup id="cite_ref-25" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-25">[25]</a></sup> The protection of its water resources made significant increases in the country's economy in less than two years.<sup id="cite_ref-26" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-26">[26]</a></sup> In 2017, the nation became the first to establish an eco-promise, known as the <i>Palau Pledge</i>, which are stamped on local and foreign passports.<sup id="cite_ref-27" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-27">[27]</a></sup> In 2018, Palau and the Philippines began re-connecting their economic and diplomatic relations. The Philippines supported Palau to become an observer state in <a href="/wiki/ASEAN" title="ASEAN">ASEAN</a>, as Palau also has Southeast Asian ethnic origins.<sup id="cite_ref-mb.com.ph_28-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-mb.com.ph-28">[28]</a></sup> </p> 
      <h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Politics_and_government">Politics and government</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Palau&amp;action=edit&amp;section=9" title="Edit section: Politics and government">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2> 
      <div role="note" class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable">
       Main article: <a href="/wiki/Politics_of_Palau" title="Politics of Palau">Politics of Palau</a>
      </div> 
      <link rel="mw-deduplicated-inline-style" href="mw-data:TemplateStyles:r992277484">
      <div class="mw-stack stack-container stack-right">
       <div>
        <div class="thumb tright">
         <div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;">
          <a href="/wiki/File:Capitol,_Melekeok,_Palau.jpg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/8/8f/Capitol%2C_Melekeok%2C_Palau.jpg/220px-Capitol%2C_Melekeok%2C_Palau.jpg" decoding="async" width="220" height="147" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/8/8f/Capitol%2C_Melekeok%2C_Palau.jpg/330px-Capitol%2C_Melekeok%2C_Palau.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/8/8f/Capitol%2C_Melekeok%2C_Palau.jpg/440px-Capitol%2C_Melekeok%2C_Palau.jpg 2x" data-file-width="3474" data-file-height="2314"></a> 
          <div class="thumbcaption">
           <div class="magnify">
            <a href="/wiki/File:Capitol,_Melekeok,_Palau.jpg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a>
           </div><a href="/wiki/Capitol_of_Palau" title="Capitol of Palau">Capitol of Palau</a>, the seat of government.
          </div>
         </div>
        </div>
       </div>
      </div> 
      <p>Palau is a <a href="/wiki/Representative_democracy" title="Representative democracy">democratic</a> <a href="/wiki/Republic" title="Republic">republic</a>. The <a href="/wiki/President_of_Palau" title="President of Palau">President of Palau</a> is both <a href="/wiki/Head_of_state" title="Head of state">head of state</a> and <a href="/wiki/Head_of_government" title="Head of government">head of government</a>. <a href="/wiki/Executive_power" class="mw-redirect" title="Executive power">Executive power</a> is exercised by the government, while <a href="/wiki/Legislative_power" class="mw-redirect" title="Legislative power">legislative power</a> is vested in both the government and the <a href="/wiki/Palau_National_Congress" title="Palau National Congress">Palau National Congress</a>. The <a href="/wiki/Judiciary_of_Palau" title="Judiciary of Palau">judiciary</a> is independent of the executive and the legislature. Palau adopted a constitution in 1981. </p>
      <p>The governments of the United States and Palau concluded a <a href="/wiki/Compact_of_Free_Association" title="Compact of Free Association">Compact of Free Association</a> in 1986, similar to compacts that the United States had entered into with the <a href="/wiki/Federated_States_of_Micronesia" title="Federated States of Micronesia">Federated States of Micronesia</a> and the <a href="/wiki/Marshall_Islands" title="Marshall Islands">Republic of the Marshall Islands</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-gao-08-732_p7_29-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-gao-08-732_p7-29">[29]</a></sup> The compact entered into force on 1 October 1994, concluding Palau's transition from trusteeship to independence<sup id="cite_ref-gao-08-732_p7_29-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-gao-08-732_p7-29">[29]</a></sup> as the last portion of the <a href="/wiki/Trust_Territory_of_the_Pacific_Islands" title="Trust Territory of the Pacific Islands">Trust Territory of the Pacific Islands</a> to secure its independence pursuant to <a href="/wiki/United_Nations_Security_Council_Resolution_956" title="United Nations Security Council Resolution 956">Security Council Resolution 956</a>. </p>
      <p>The <a href="/wiki/Compact_of_Free_Association" title="Compact of Free Association">Compact of Free Association</a> between the United States and Palau<sup id="cite_ref-30" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-30">[30]</a></sup> sets forth the free and voluntary association of their governments. It primarily focuses on the issues of government, economic, security and defense relations.<sup id="cite_ref-31" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-31">[31]</a></sup> Palau has no independent military, relying on the United States for its defense. Under the compact, the <a href="/wiki/American_military" class="mw-redirect" title="American military">American military</a> was granted access to the islands for 50 years. The <a href="/wiki/United_States_Navy" title="United States Navy">U.S. Navy</a> role is minimal, limited to a handful of Navy <a href="/wiki/Seabee_(US_Navy)" class="mw-redirect" title="Seabee (US Navy)">Seabees</a> (construction engineers).<sup class="noprint Inline-Template Template-Fact" style="white-space:nowrap;">[<i><a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Citation_needed" title="Wikipedia:Citation needed"><span title="This claim needs references to reliable sources. (August 2019)">citation needed</span></a></i>]</sup> The <a href="/wiki/United_States_Coast_Guard" title="United States Coast Guard">U.S. Coast Guard</a> patrols in national waters. </p> 
      <h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Foreign_relations">Foreign relations</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Palau&amp;action=edit&amp;section=10" title="Edit section: Foreign relations">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3> 
      <div role="note" class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable">
       Main article: <a href="/wiki/Foreign_relations_of_Palau" title="Foreign relations of Palau">Foreign relations of Palau</a>
      </div> 
      <link rel="mw-deduplicated-inline-style" href="mw-data:TemplateStyles:r992277484">
      <div class="mw-stack stack-container stack-right">
       <div>
        <div class="thumb tright">
         <div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;">
          <a href="/wiki/File:%E7%B8%BD%E7%B5%B1%E6%8E%A5%E5%8F%97%E5%B8%9B%E7%90%89%E5%85%B1%E5%92%8C%E5%9C%8B%E7%B8%BD%E7%B5%B1%E9%9B%B7%E8%92%99%E5%82%91%E7%B4%A2(Tommy_E._Remengesau,_Jr.)_%E8%B4%88%E7%A6%AE_(27163347055).jpg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/67/%E7%B8%BD%E7%B5%B1%E6%8E%A5%E5%8F%97%E5%B8%9B%E7%90%89%E5%85%B1%E5%92%8C%E5%9C%8B%E7%B8%BD%E7%B5%B1%E9%9B%B7%E8%92%99%E5%82%91%E7%B4%A2%28Tommy_E._Remengesau%2C_Jr.%29_%E8%B4%88%E7%A6%AE_%2827163347055%29.jpg/220px-%E7%B8%BD%E7%B5%B1%E6%8E%A5%E5%8F%97%E5%B8%9B%E7%90%89%E5%85%B1%E5%92%8C%E5%9C%8B%E7%B8%BD%E7%B5%B1%E9%9B%B7%E8%92%99%E5%82%91%E7%B4%A2%28Tommy_E._Remengesau%2C_Jr.%29_%E8%B4%88%E7%A6%AE_%2827163347055%29.jpg" decoding="async" width="220" height="157" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/67/%E7%B8%BD%E7%B5%B1%E6%8E%A5%E5%8F%97%E5%B8%9B%E7%90%89%E5%85%B1%E5%92%8C%E5%9C%8B%E7%B8%BD%E7%B5%B1%E9%9B%B7%E8%92%99%E5%82%91%E7%B4%A2%28Tommy_E._Remengesau%2C_Jr.%29_%E8%B4%88%E7%A6%AE_%2827163347055%29.jpg/330px-%E7%B8%BD%E7%B5%B1%E6%8E%A5%E5%8F%97%E5%B8%9B%E7%90%89%E5%85%B1%E5%92%8C%E5%9C%8B%E7%B8%BD%E7%B5%B1%E9%9B%B7%E8%92%99%E5%82%91%E7%B4%A2%28Tommy_E._Remengesau%2C_Jr.%29_%E8%B4%88%E7%A6%AE_%2827163347055%29.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/67/%E7%B8%BD%E7%B5%B1%E6%8E%A5%E5%8F%97%E5%B8%9B%E7%90%89%E5%85%B1%E5%92%8C%E5%9C%8B%E7%B8%BD%E7%B5%B1%E9%9B%B7%E8%92%99%E5%82%91%E7%B4%A2%28Tommy_E._Remengesau%2C_Jr.%29_%E8%B4%88%E7%A6%AE_%2827163347055%29.jpg/440px-%E7%B8%BD%E7%B5%B1%E6%8E%A5%E5%8F%97%E5%B8%9B%E7%90%89%E5%85%B1%E5%92%8C%E5%9C%8B%E7%B8%BD%E7%B5%B1%E9%9B%B7%E8%92%99%E5%82%91%E7%B4%A2%28Tommy_E._Remengesau%2C_Jr.%29_%E8%B4%88%E7%A6%AE_%2827163347055%29.jpg 2x" data-file-width="3150" data-file-height="2250"></a> 
          <div class="thumbcaption">
           <div class="magnify">
            <a href="/wiki/File:%E7%B8%BD%E7%B5%B1%E6%8E%A5%E5%8F%97%E5%B8%9B%E7%90%89%E5%85%B1%E5%92%8C%E5%9C%8B%E7%B8%BD%E7%B5%B1%E9%9B%B7%E8%92%99%E5%82%91%E7%B4%A2(Tommy_E._Remengesau,_Jr.)_%E8%B4%88%E7%A6%AE_(27163347055).jpg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a>
           </div>President <a href="/wiki/Thomas_Remengesau_Jr." title="Thomas Remengesau Jr.">Thomas Remengesau</a> with the <a href="/wiki/Taiwan" title="Taiwan">Republic of China (Taiwan)'s</a> President <a href="/wiki/Tsai_Ing-wen" title="Tsai Ing-wen">Tsai Ing-wen</a> in 2016.
          </div>
         </div>
        </div>
       </div>
      </div> 
      <p>As a sovereign nation, Palau conducts its own foreign relations.<sup id="cite_ref-gao-08-732_p7_29-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-gao-08-732_p7-29">[29]</a></sup> Since independence, Palau has established diplomatic relations with a number of nations, including many of its Pacific neighbors, like <a href="/wiki/Federated_States_of_Micronesia" title="Federated States of Micronesia">Micronesia</a> and the <a href="/wiki/Philippines" title="Philippines">Philippines</a>. On 29 November 1994, the <a href="/wiki/United_Nations_Security_Council" title="United Nations Security Council">United Nations Security Council</a> passed <a href="/wiki/United_Nations_Security_Council_Resolution_963" title="United Nations Security Council Resolution 963">Resolution 963</a> recommending Palau's admission to the <a href="/wiki/United_Nations" title="United Nations">United Nations</a>. The <a href="/wiki/United_Nations_General_Assembly" title="United Nations General Assembly">United Nations General Assembly</a> approved admission for Palau pursuant to Resolution 49/63 on 15 December 1994.<sup id="cite_ref-32" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-32">[32]</a></sup> Palau has since joined several other international organizations. In September 2006, Palau hosted the first <a href="/wiki/Taiwan" title="Taiwan">Taiwan</a>-Pacific Allies Summit. Its President has made official visits to other Pacific countries, including Japan.<sup id="cite_ref-33" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-33">[33]</a></sup> </p>
      <p>The United States maintains a diplomatic delegation and an <a href="/wiki/Embassy" class="mw-redirect" title="Embassy">embassy</a> in Palau, but most aspects of the countries' relationship have to do with Compact-funded projects, which are the responsibility of the U.S. <a href="/wiki/Department_of_the_Interior" class="mw-redirect" title="Department of the Interior">Department of the Interior</a>'s <a href="/wiki/Office_of_Insular_Affairs" title="Office of Insular Affairs">Office of Insular Affairs</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-34" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-34">[34]</a></sup> For example, as part of this Compact, Palau was granted <a href="/wiki/ZIP_Code" title="ZIP Code">zip codes</a> 96939 and 96940, along with regular <a href="/wiki/United_States_Postal_Service" title="United States Postal Service">US Mail</a> delivery. </p>
      <p>In international politics, Palau often votes with the United States on <a href="/wiki/United_Nations_General_Assembly" title="United Nations General Assembly">United Nations General Assembly</a> resolutions.<sup id="cite_ref-35" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-35">[35]</a></sup> </p>
      <p>Palau has maintained close ties with Japan, which has funded infrastructure projects including the <a href="/wiki/Koror%E2%80%93Babeldaob_Bridge" title="Koror–Babeldaob Bridge">Koror–Babeldaob Bridge</a>. In 2015, Emperor <a href="/wiki/Akihito" title="Akihito">Akihito</a> and <a href="/wiki/Empress_Michiko" title="Empress Michiko">Empress Michiko</a> visited <a href="/wiki/Peleliu" title="Peleliu">Peleliu</a> to honor the 70th anniversary of <a href="/wiki/World_War_II" title="World War II">World War II</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-36" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-36">[36]</a></sup> </p>
      <p>Palau is a member of the <a href="/wiki/Nauru_Agreement" title="Nauru Agreement">Nauru Agreement</a> for the Management of Fisheries.<sup id="cite_ref-radioaustralia_37-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-radioaustralia-37">[37]</a></sup> </p> 
      <link rel="mw-deduplicated-inline-style" href="mw-data:TemplateStyles:r992277484">
      <div class="mw-stack stack-container stack-right">
       <div>
        <div class="thumb tright">
         <div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;">
          <a href="/wiki/File:Palau_Pres_Thomas_Remengesau_with_PH_President_Rodrigo_Duterte.jpg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/62/Palau_Pres_Thomas_Remengesau_with_PH_President_Rodrigo_Duterte.jpg/220px-Palau_Pres_Thomas_Remengesau_with_PH_President_Rodrigo_Duterte.jpg" decoding="async" width="220" height="147" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/62/Palau_Pres_Thomas_Remengesau_with_PH_President_Rodrigo_Duterte.jpg/330px-Palau_Pres_Thomas_Remengesau_with_PH_President_Rodrigo_Duterte.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/62/Palau_Pres_Thomas_Remengesau_with_PH_President_Rodrigo_Duterte.jpg/440px-Palau_Pres_Thomas_Remengesau_with_PH_President_Rodrigo_Duterte.jpg 2x" data-file-width="2400" data-file-height="1600"></a> 
          <div class="thumbcaption">
           <div class="magnify">
            <a href="/wiki/File:Palau_Pres_Thomas_Remengesau_with_PH_President_Rodrigo_Duterte.jpg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a>
           </div>President Remengesau with Philippine President <a href="/wiki/Rodrigo_Duterte" title="Rodrigo Duterte">Rodrigo Duterte</a> in 2018.
          </div>
         </div>
        </div>
       </div>
      </div> 
      <p>In 1981, Palau voted for the world's first nuclear-free constitution. This constitution banned the use, storage and disposal of <a href="/wiki/Nuclear_weapon" title="Nuclear weapon">nuclear</a>, <a href="/wiki/Chemical_weapon" title="Chemical weapon">toxic chemical</a>, gas and <a href="/wiki/Biological_weapon" class="mw-redirect" title="Biological weapon">biological weapons</a> without first being approved by a <style data-mw-deduplicate="TemplateStyles:r1020198016">.mw-parser-output .frac{white-space:nowrap}.mw-parser-output .frac .num,.mw-parser-output .frac .den{font-size:80%;line-height:0;vertical-align:super}.mw-parser-output .frac .den{vertical-align:sub}.mw-parser-output .sr-only{border:0;clip:rect(0,0,0,0);height:1px;margin:-1px;overflow:hidden;padding:0;position:absolute;width:1px}</style><span class="frac" role="math"><span class="num">3</span>⁄<span class="den">4</span></span>, or 75 percent, majority in a referendum.<sup id="cite_ref-38" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-38">[38]</a></sup> This ban delayed Palau's transition to independence, because while negotiating the Compact, the U.S. insisted on the option to operate <a href="/wiki/Nuclear_marine_propulsion" title="Nuclear marine propulsion">nuclear propelled vessels</a> and store nuclear weapons within the territory,<sup id="cite_ref-39" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-39">[39]</a></sup> prompting campaigns for independence and denuclearisation.<sup id="cite_ref-40" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-40">[40]</a></sup> After several referendums that failed to achieve a ¾ majority, the people of Palau finally approved the Compact in 1994.<sup id="cite_ref-41" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-41">[41]</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-42" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-42">[42]</a></sup> </p>
      <p>The <a href="/wiki/Philippines" title="Philippines">Philippines</a>, a neighboring ally of Palau to the west, has expressed its intent to back Palau if ever it wishes to join <a href="/wiki/Association_of_Southeast_Asian_Nations" class="mw-redirect" title="Association of Southeast Asian Nations">ASEAN</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-mb.com.ph_28-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-mb.com.ph-28">[28]</a></sup> </p>
      <p>In June 2009, Palau announced that it would <a href="/wiki/Uyghur_captives_in_Guantanamo" class="mw-redirect" title="Uyghur captives in Guantanamo">accept up to seventeen</a> <a href="/wiki/Uyghurs" title="Uyghurs">Uyghurs</a> who had previously been detained by the American military at <a href="/wiki/Guantanamo_Bay_detention_camp" title="Guantanamo Bay detention camp">Guantanamo Bay</a>,<sup id="cite_ref-Ctv2009-06-10_43-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Ctv2009-06-10-43">[43]</a></sup> with some American compensation for the cost of their upkeep.<sup id="cite_ref-Abc2009-06-10_44-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Abc2009-06-10-44">[44]</a></sup> </p>
      <p>Only one of the Uyghurs initially agreed to resettlement,<sup id="cite_ref-Rnzi2009-06-30_45-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Rnzi2009-06-30-45">[45]</a></sup> but by the end of October, six of the seventeen had been transferred to Palau.<sup id="cite_ref-Afp2009-10-31_46-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Afp2009-10-31-46">[46]</a></sup> An aid agreement with the United States, finalized in January 2010, was reported to be unrelated to the Uyghur agreement.<sup id="cite_ref-47" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-47">[47]</a></sup> </p>
      <p>In 2017, Palau signed the United Nations <a href="/wiki/Treaty_on_the_Prohibition_of_Nuclear_Weapons" title="Treaty on the Prohibition of Nuclear Weapons">Treaty on the Prohibition of Nuclear Weapons</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-48" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-48">[48]</a></sup> </p> 
      <h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Administrative_divisions">Administrative divisions</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Palau&amp;action=edit&amp;section=11" title="Edit section: Administrative divisions">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3> 
      <div role="note" class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable">
       Main article: <a href="/wiki/States_of_Palau" title="States of Palau">States of Palau</a>
      </div>

         <td>Angaur Island, 12&nbsp;km south of Peleliu </td>
        </tr> 
        <tr> 
         <td><a href="/wiki/File:Flag_of_Sonsorol.svg" class="image"><img alt="Flag of Sonsorol.svg" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/0/01/Flag_of_Sonsorol.svg/27px-Flag_of_Sonsorol.svg.png" decoding="async" width="27" height="16" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/0/01/Flag_of_Sonsorol.svg/41px-Flag_of_Sonsorol.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/0/01/Flag_of_Sonsorol.svg/54px-Flag_of_Sonsorol.svg.png 2x" data-file-width="361" data-file-height="216"></a> <a href="/wiki/Sonsorol" title="Sonsorol">Sonsorol</a> </td>

         <td style="text-align:right;">42 </td> 
         <td style="text-align:right;">40 </td> 
         <td>comprises Sonsorol, <a href="/wiki/Fana_Island" title="Fana Island">Fanna</a>, Pulo Anna and <a href="/wiki/Merir" title="Merir">Merir</a> Islands </td>
        </tr> 
        <tr> 
         <td><a href="/wiki/File:Flag_of_Hatohobei.svg" class="image"><img alt="Flag of Hatohobei.svg" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/e/e9/Flag_of_Hatohobei.svg/27px-Flag_of_Hatohobei.svg.png" decoding="async" width="27" height="17" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/e/e9/Flag_of_Hatohobei.svg/41px-Flag_of_Hatohobei.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/e/e9/Flag_of_Hatohobei.svg/54px-Flag_of_Hatohobei.svg.png 2x" data-file-width="800" data-file-height="500"></a> <a href="/wiki/Hatohobei" title="Hatohobei">Hatohobei</a> </td> 
         <td style="text-align:right;">0.9 </td> 
         <td style="text-align:right;">10 </td> 
         <td style="text-align:right;">25 </td> 
         <td>comprises <a href="/wiki/Tobi_(island)" title="Tobi (island)">Tobi Island</a> and (uninhabited) Helen Reef </td>
        </tr>
       </tbody>
      </table> 
      <p>Historically, Palau's <a href="/wiki/Rock_Islands_(Palau)" class="mw-redirect" title="Rock Islands (Palau)">Rock Islands</a> have been part of the State of Koror. The Southwestern islands (Sonsorol and Hatohobei States) do not speak <a href="/wiki/Palauan" class="mw-redirect" title="Palauan">Palauan</a>, but the distantly related <a href="/wiki/Sonsorolese_language" title="Sonsorolese language">Sonsorolese</a>-<a href="/wiki/Tobian_language" title="Tobian language">Tobian</a> (related to <a href="/wiki/Woleaian_language" title="Woleaian language">Woleaian</a> of <a href="/wiki/Woleai" title="Woleai">Woleai</a> atoll, <a href="/wiki/Yap_State" title="Yap State">Yap State</a>) </p> 
      <h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Maritime_law_enforcement">Maritime law enforcement</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Palau&amp;action=edit&amp;section=12" title="Edit section: Maritime law enforcement">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3> 
      <div class="thumb tright">
       <div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;">
        <a href="/wiki/File:Palau_Maritime_Police_vessel.jpg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/b/ba/Palau_Maritime_Police_vessel.jpg/220px-Palau_Maritime_Police_vessel.jpg" decoding="async" width="220" height="147" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/b/ba/Palau_Maritime_Police_vessel.jpg/330px-Palau_Maritime_Police_vessel.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/b/ba/Palau_Maritime_Police_vessel.jpg/440px-Palau_Maritime_Police_vessel.jpg 2x" data-file-width="2250" data-file-height="1500"></a> 
        <div class="thumbcaption">
         <div class="magnify">
          <a href="/wiki/File:Palau_Maritime_Police_vessel.jpg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a>
         </div>The <i><a href="/wiki/Euatel" title="Euatel">Euatel</a></i>, <i><a href="/w/index.php?title=Kabekl_M%E2%80%99tal&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="Kabekl M’tal (page does not exist)">Kabekl M’tal</a></i> and <i><a href="/w/index.php?title=PPS_Bul&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="PPS Bul (page does not exist)">Bul</a></i> provide littoral fishery protection.<sup id="cite_ref-IslandTimes2017-04-25_49-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-IslandTimes2017-04-25-49">[49]</a></sup>
        </div>
       </div>
      </div> 
      <p>Palau's <a href="/wiki/Division_of_Marine_Law_Enforcement" class="mw-redirect" title="Division of Marine Law Enforcement">Division of Marine Law Enforcement</a> patrols the nation's 600,000 square kilometers (230,000 square miles) <a href="/wiki/Exclusive_economic_zone" title="Exclusive economic zone">exclusive economic zone</a>. They operate two long range patrol boats, the <i><a href="/wiki/Kedam" class="mw-redirect" title="Kedam">Kedam</a></i> and the <i><a href="/wiki/PSS_Remeliik_II" title="PSS Remeliik II">Remeliik II</a></i>, to hunt for poachers and unlicensed fishermen.<sup id="cite_ref-PacificNote2017-12-22_50-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-PacificNote2017-12-22-50">[50]</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-PalauPresident2017-05-08_51-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-PalauPresident2017-05-08-51">[51]</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-PostGuam2016-03-03_52-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-PostGuam2016-03-03-52">[52]</a></sup> Smaller boats are used for littoral operations.<sup id="cite_ref-IslandTimes2017-04-25_49-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-IslandTimes2017-04-25-49">[49]</a></sup> They are based on <a href="/wiki/Koror" title="Koror">Koror</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-53" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-53">[53]</a></sup> </p> 
      <h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Geography">Geography</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Palau&amp;action=edit&amp;section=13" title="Edit section: Geography">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2> 
      <div role="note" class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable">
       Main article: <a href="/wiki/Geography_of_Palau" title="Geography of Palau">Geography of Palau</a>
      </div> 
      <p>Palau's territory consists of an archipelago located in the <a href="/wiki/Pacific_Ocean" title="Pacific Ocean">Pacific Ocean</a>. Its most populous <a href="/wiki/Island" title="Island">islands</a> are <a href="/wiki/Angaur" title="Angaur">Angaur</a>, <a href="/wiki/Babeldaob" title="Babeldaob">Babeldaob</a>, <a href="/wiki/Koror" title="Koror">Koror</a> and <a href="/wiki/Peleliu" title="Peleliu">Peleliu</a>. The latter three lie together within the same <a href="/wiki/Coral_reef" title="Coral reef">barrier reef</a>, while Angaur is an oceanic island several kilometers to the south. About two-thirds of the <a href="/wiki/Population" title="Population">population</a> lives on Koror. </p>
      <p>The <a href="/wiki/Coral" title="Coral">coral</a> <a href="/wiki/Atoll" title="Atoll">atoll</a> of <a href="/wiki/Kayangel" title="Kayangel">Kayangel</a> is north of these islands, while the uninhabited <a href="/wiki/Rock_Islands_(Palau)" class="mw-redirect" title="Rock Islands (Palau)">Rock Islands</a> (about 200) are west of the main island group. A remote group of six islands, known as the <a href="/wiki/Southwest_Islands_(Palau)" title="Southwest Islands (Palau)">Southwest Islands</a>, some 604 kilometers (375 miles) from the main islands, make up the states of Hatohobei and Sonsorol. </p> 
      <h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Climate">Climate</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Palau&amp;action=edit&amp;section=14" title="Edit section: Climate">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3> 
      <p>Palau has a <a href="/wiki/Tropical_rainforest_climate" title="Tropical rainforest climate">tropical rainforest climate</a> with an annual <a href="/wiki/Arithmetic_mean" title="Arithmetic mean">mean</a> <a href="/wiki/Temperature" title="Temperature">temperature</a> of 28&nbsp;°C (82&nbsp;°F). <a href="/wiki/Rainfall" class="mw-redirect" title="Rainfall">Rainfall</a> is heavy throughout the <a href="/wiki/Year" title="Year">year</a>, averaging 3,800&nbsp;mm (150&nbsp;in). The average <a href="/wiki/Humidity" title="Humidity">humidity</a> is 82% and, although rain falls more frequently between July and October, there is still much <a href="/wiki/Sunlight" title="Sunlight">sunshine</a>. </p>
      <p>Palau lies on the edge of the typhoon belt. Tropical disturbances frequently develop near Palau every year, but significant <a href="/wiki/Tropical_cyclone" title="Tropical cyclone">tropical cyclones</a> are quite rare. <a href="/wiki/Typhoon_Mike" title="Typhoon Mike">Mike</a>, <a href="/wiki/Typhoon_Bopha" title="Typhoon Bopha">Bopha</a> and <a href="/wiki/Typhoon_Haiyan" title="Typhoon Haiyan">Haiyan</a> are the only systems that struck Palau as <a href="/wiki/Typhoon" title="Typhoon">typhoons</a> on record.<sup id="cite_ref-54" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-54">[54]</a></sup> </p> 
      <div style="clear:both;"></div>

      <h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Environment">Environment</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Palau&amp;action=edit&amp;section=15" title="Edit section: Environment">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3> 
      <div class="thumb tright">
